(Calcutta) There were two earthquakes in Durbari, Hazara District, Northwest Frontier Province, British India, today, which were quite severe. Residents were greatly alarmed. The statue of Queen Victoria and some houses were destroyed, but no injuries were reported. (1st Reuters Dispatch)

Regarding the Italian-Abyssinian Dispute, Britain and France Are Working Hard to Mediate; Hoare and Laval Will Meet to Discuss a Peaceful Solution 58

(London) According to observations by political figures here, the Italian-Abyssinian dispute will have an important development in the middle of next week, or even be decisive. The French government will submit the minimum settlement conditions drafted by Britain and France to the Italian Prime Minister, and Mussolini will reply to them. It is generally believed that Sanderson, the Abyssinian problem expert of the British Foreign Office, has been instructed to wait for the Italian reply in the French capital, so as to compare the conditions drafted by Britain and France. People here still hope that Foreign Secretary Sir Samuel Hoare will meet with French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval within the next few days and decide on the common attitude of Britain and France on the issue of oil embargo and the minimum conditions for Italian reconciliation. Regarding the oil embargo issue, the 18-nation committee is now scheduled to meet on December 12 to discuss it. Some people speculate that after the oil embargo measures are passed by the Sanctions Adjustment Committee, the date of its implementation may not be decided immediately, so that the ongoing negotiations between Britain, France and Italy can continue without being affected. In addition, the staff reporter also said that when Hoare and Laval meet in the future, they will also discuss the issue of Germany returning to the League of Nations and the air force, and both parties will reach an agreement. Regarding this issue, the British Foreign Office has sent Colonel Evers to Berlin several times and is still there. (30th Havas Dispatch)

(Paris) According to information obtained by the company's diplomatic staff reporter, Premier and Foreign Minister Laval is extremely willing to meet with British Foreign Secretary Samuel Hoare before the 18-nation committee decides to implement the oil embargo measures, so as to jointly formulate a proposal to resolve the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, and which can be accepted by the Italian government before the League of Nations implements the oil embargo. It is now heard that the British government has also expressed its approval of the meeting between the diplomatic authorities of Britain and France, and the date of the meeting is also under consideration by both parties. Premier Laval initially intended to go to London in person to attend the opening of the London Naval Conference, so as to take the opportunity to exchange opinions with the British authorities on the Italian-Abyssinian issue. If not, Hoare may make a brief stop in the French capital on his way to Geneva to participate in the 18-nation committee, so that he can meet with Laval. If the above two methods are not possible, Laval and Hoare will be able to meet in Geneva when the 18-nation committee meets on December 12. At that time, it will not hurt to take the opportunity to discuss various outstanding issues. As for the statement issued by the Italian authorities yesterday on the oil embargo measures, saying that it will be regarded as an unfriendly move rather than a hostile act, French officials were quite satisfied when they heard it. In short, what the French government has always been concerned about is to make every effort to localize the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, and to try to avoid adopting oil embargo measures within the possible range. In addition, the French government is also eager for the talks between Sanderson, the British Foreign Office expert on Abyssinian issues, and Saint Quentin, the director of the African Department of the French Foreign Office, to be accelerated in order to formulate proposals that can be accepted by all parties. However, the British expert Sanderson has recently been ordered to return home before the establishment of a mutually agreed solution, so the talks between the two parties have to be temporarily suspended. As for the proposals currently being considered by the two experts Sanderson and Saint Quentin, it is heard that they are very similar to those drafted in October. However, at that time, they were once put on hold because they failed to obtain the approval of the League of Nations and the three parties of Italy, Abyssinia. It is now planned that Abyssinia will cede some territory to Italy, and other land will be ceded to Abyssinia to enable Abyssinia to obtain access to the sea in exchange for the territory of Abyssinia obtained by Italy, the main one being the southern Ogaden region. However, the proposal to divide Abyssinia's headquarters and frontier provinces into two seems to be opposed by the League of Nations and the Abyssinian Emperor, and even the cession of Tigre Province is not allowed. In addition, there are general plans, including the conclusion of a treaty to provide assistance to Abyssinia under the supervision of the League of Nations, which is one aspect. It is heard that the French government now hopes that the Italian government can take into account the views of all parties and put forward its own plans. If so, the ingredients for resolving the Italian-Abyssinian dispute can be gradually increased, and the proposal for an oil embargo may also be postponed. However, the Italian proposal must be submitted before the 18-nation committee meets. If not, once the oil embargo is passed by the committee, an order will be issued immediately. This is why French Premier and Foreign Minister Laval is eager for Britain and France to continue their efforts to mediate and wants to meet with British Foreign Secretary Hoare as soon as possible. (1st Havas News Agency Dispatch)

Ethiopian Guerrilla Warfare Repeatedly Achieves Victory 66

Asmara: The Italian vanguard attempting to occupy the Danakil Highlands is now greatly troubled by the defensive army's guerrilla tactics. General Siyoum's troops are now divided into countless small units, each with about a hundred men, containing the advance of two Italian divisions in the east and one Italian division in the north. These troops often threaten the Italian lines of communication and launch surprise attacks from the rear of the Italian army. Amari, the main general under Siyoum, has apparently taken on the task of defending Dambian. Siyoum himself plans to join forces with General Gaza's troops. Amari is skilled in guerrilla warfare and can often conceal his troops so that they are not seen by Italian planes. The Italian army initially tried to encircle and penetrate the jungles of Dambian, but failed. Therefore, they are now launching a full-scale offensive, but the Ethiopian soldiers are familiar with the terrain, skilled in guerrilla warfare, and do not make direct contact. (1st Reuters Telegram)

Italy Expands: The Highest National Defense Authority. Recruiting Personnel from Various Ministries to Participate in Active Preparation for Future Wars. Routine Winter Rotation of Troops at Headquarters 67

(Rome) Today, the State Council has amended the organizational law of the Supreme National Defense Committee to become a national representative body to cope with war, including deliberative committees and various advisory committees. The deliberative committee is chaired by Prime Minister Mussolini himself, and all cabinet members participate (the ministers of justice, education, and propaganda information have just joined). The various advisory committees were originally organized by the Chief of General Staff, the General Secretary of the Fascist Party, and the Chiefs of Staff of the Army, Navy, and Air Force. From now on, the generals of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, the Chief of Staff of the Party Army, and the Director-General of Military Training will all join. The Supreme National Defense Committee was established on January 7, 1923, with the aim of concentrating national strength to build national defense and prepare for future wars. Its responsibilities are not only military in nature. (30th Havas Telegram)

(Paris) Regarding the secret troop movements in Italy, reliable sources have reported that the troops stationed on the Italian-Austrian border must be returned to their original defensive positions for the winter. These troops, totaling 500,000, were transferred to the Brenner Pass on the Italian-Austrian border in August after the army's large-scale maneuvers. Now that winter has arrived, the climate in the area is harsh, and most of the troops are not accustomed to it, so it is necessary to transfer them away. As for the Italian-French border, the number of Italian troops stationed there remains the same as before, and there is no large concentration of troops. (30th Havas Telegram)

(Rome) Regarding the secret troop movements in Italy, this newspaper's reporter declares that there has been no increase in the number of Italian troops stationed on the French border. Only a few battalions of soldiers were previously transferred to other locations to participate in exercises, and have recently been returned to their original defenses. The current number of troops on the French border is not only no more than it was during the large-scale maneuvers in August of this year, but is actually less. For example, the "Cosselia Division" and the "Asieta Division" were ordered to go to the Libyan colony in Africa. So far, only the "Cosselia Division" has been transferred back to its original defenses, and the defensive positions left by the "Asieta Division" have not been fully filled. In addition, the government's newly formed motorized troop, the "Toranto Division," is not near the French border either. (1st Havas Telegram)

Italian Army Changes War Strategy 68

Addis Ababa: This newspaper's reporter, O. This area is barren, sparsely populated, and has a harsh climate. Only the fierce Asseymara tribe, led by Chief Yayout, roams there. The chief has been appointed as the commander-in-chief of the eastern route by Ethiopian General Gaitatchu. Japan Refreshes Diplomatic Lineup: Ministry of Foreign Affairs Adds South Seas Section 74

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has been granted a new budget request of over 12 million yen and plans to refresh its diplomatic lineup from the new year. The establishment of a South Seas Section is particularly noteworthy. The main new facilities are as follows:

(1) The Trade Bureau will establish a new General Affairs Section. The proposal for an external bureau of the Trade Bureau has been rejected, so a new General Affairs Section will be established to unify and comprehensively handle the affairs of the various sections of the Trade Bureau. The section chief will be a Choku-nin rank official acting as or assisting the bureau director. (1) A new Third Eurasia Section will be established to manage affairs related to the Dutch East Indies, the Straits Settlements, Borneo, India, Burma, New Zealand, and Australia. Active efforts will be made to promote goodwill in these regions. (1) A new Accounting Officer will be established. In light of the Mogi incident in Qingdao, this officer will be established to ensure the strictness of the accounting system. (1) A new Academic Affairs Officer will be established to educate the children of Japanese expatriates overseas. They will be first dispatched to Changchun and Rio de Janeiro. (1) The Ministry will establish new Telegraph Officers and Assistant Officers to research and improve codes and ciphers. (1) A new embassy will be established in Finland. (1) Consulates will be added in Mudanjiang, Jiamusi, Shanhaiguan, and Dolon. (1st Den-tsu Telegram)

Soviet Union Cracks International Spy Agency: Specialized in Spying on the Secrets of the Red Army, Leader Shot Dead on the Spot During Arrest 75

Leningrad: The Soviet Union recently crushed a large-scale spy organization. This organization was run by the Estonian Intelligence Group, and its founder was Geivisak, an agent of the group. Geivisak illegally entered Soviet territory. On September 19, the authorities in the Ratske County of the Pskov Province attempted to arrest Geivisak. Geivisak resisted with weapons and killed a messenger of the Pskov Provincial Office of the People's Commissariat for Internal Affairs. In the resulting firefight, Geivisak was also killed. Two pistols, one hundred packs of ammunition, Estonian and Soviet currency, and a collection of espionage materials were found on his person. In connection with this case, several of Geivisak's subordinates were arrested in the Ratske District, the Luga District, and Leningrad, including five Estonian citizens of Soviet origin who directly assisted Geivisak. The spy ring was engaged in collecting classified documents of the Red Army and military police in the Leningrad, Luga, Novgorod, and Pskov provinces. The ring included Geivisak's relatives and wealthy White Guard peasants. They joined the ring when they were conscripted into the Red Army or served in the Red Army. The case is still under investigation. (1st Tass Telegram)

Greek King Orders General Amnesty for Political Prisoners: Confiscated Property to Be Returned in Full; New Prime Minister Announces Policy Outline 76

Athens: King George of Greece will issue a decree of amnesty for political prisoners, both civilian and military, to commemorate his restoration to the throne. According to Mr. Demetzis, the new prime minister who took office yesterday, this order will be issued tomorrow, and the confiscated property of each person will be returned. However, former military officers will not be reinstated. The Prime Minister also issued a statement yesterday, saying that the new government will implement a policy of national harmony and reconstruction, the procedures are as follows, free elections, budgetary thrift, strengthening national defense, strict adherence to international treaties, adhering to the Balkan Pact, improving diplomatic relations. Former Prime Minister General Kondylis resigned in anger due to differences of opinion with the King of Greece regarding the amnesty of political prisoners. (1st Reuters Telegram)

Athens: The new Prime Minister Demetzis recently issued a statement to the press, saying, "The new government is a government dedicated to construction work in the spirit of national harmony. Its political program can be summarized in the following four points: (1) free elections, (2) thrifty budget, (3) strengthening national defense, (4) faithfully abiding by international agreements and the Balkan Pact, and treating all countries with sincere friendship, especially those countries that have historical connections with Greece and are geographically connected by land and sea." Demetzis also said that the new government is not a party cabinet, but a transitional cabinet whose purpose is to remove obstacles in the political situation so that the next government elected by the people can work smoothly. (1st Havas Telegram)

Egyptian Independence Movement 77

Cairo, Egypt: The Egyptian Nationalist Party has decided to resume its propaganda campaign to demand the restoration of the 1923 constitution. The necessary funds will be raised through fundraising. Some people also believe that the Nationalist Party should organize a delegation to go to Geneva to explain the content of the Egyptian issue to the League of Nations. (30th Havas Telegram)

Cairo, Egypt: The leader of the Nationalist Party, Nahas, gave a speech to Egyptian university students last night, saying, "The various attempts to bring the various Egyptian political parties closer together are all directed by London. Creating and maintaining internal unrest in Egypt is in Britain's interest. We must know that under the current situation in Egypt, the Nationalist Party is the only party that can represent the national ideas." More than 1,000 university students at the scene cheered Nahas and expressed their unanimous willingness to continue the struggle as political parties. There had been attempts to reach a compromise on the constitutional issue and formulate a common political program. Nahas's speech shows that these attempts have failed. (1st Havas Telegram)

Austria Organizes Civil Corps: Deputy Prime Minister Serves as Supreme Commander 78

(Vienna) The government is currently organizing a civil corps (reorganized from the Internal Defense Corps). Colonel Kubisa, Chief of Staff of the 1st Army Division, will assume the position of Chief of General Staff of the Civil Corps next Monday and will be assisted by active-duty army officers. The Supreme Commander of the Civil Corps will still be Prince Stahrenberg, the Deputy Prime Minister. A special military officer will be responsible for liaison between the administrative affairs of the Civil Corps and the administrative affairs of the Army. (30th Havas Telegram)

German Government Officials: Fundraising to Organize Winter Relief, To Be Held on the 7th of This Month 79

In Berlin alone, more than 500,000 marks were raised. (1st Havas Telegram)

Scientific Miscellany 80

— Edited by the Chinese Science Society

Moon Embracing (Part 1) 81

— Zhang Yuzhe

In ancient times, a person from the state of Qi worried that the sky would collapse and fall, to the point of neglecting sleep and forgetting meals. After someone explained the matter to him, he was somewhat relieved. We now always think we are much smarter than the ancients, and after reading Lie Yukou's great discussion, we certainly no longer engage in such pointless "Qi worries." However, recently various newspapers have published a news story about the moon about to fall to Earth, supposedly based on the opinion of a certain astronomer. As such, readers may find it hard not to believe.

Amidst this atmosphere of fear and suspicion, with the added threat of celestial phenomena on top of human affairs, it is truly unfortunate. Although we astronomers do not have the authority to force students back to school or order citizens to stop moving, we should help dispel the rumors and fulfill our national duty. Everyone surely believes that if the moon really did fall, we astronomers would find a way to help everyone, and there's no need to panic each other. When the time comes, we will certainly not lightly speak of sacrifice, but first, let's do this initial work of dispelling rumors.

Regarding the news of the moon falling, even if it is indeed a conversation by an astronomer and not just rumors in the newspapers, there is no need to take it too seriously. In fact, apart from solar eclipses, lunar eclipses, vernal equinoxes, autumnal equinoxes, and the like, the predictions of astronomers are not necessarily much better than those of street fortune-tellers. How do we know? We have Bai Juyi's poem as proof:

Human affairs are so varied, what is there to be surprised about?

Even celestial phenomena, though considered reliable, are still often wrong.

The moon leaves the constellation of Bi, promising heavy rain,

But sometimes it doesn't rain; who can predict it?

For those who believe in the past and doubt the present, we can more easily prove that the moon falling is nothing to fear. In Zhang Zai's "Western Inscription," there is the phrase "Heaven calls itself Father, Earth calls itself Mother," which shows that the Earth is truly the mother of all things. There is no need to search for the word "Mother Earth" only in crab-walking literature. The Jade Rabbit is the most common name for the moon. As the name suggests, if the moon falls, and we were to describe it in the style of vernacular poetry, wouldn't we call it a white rabbit throwing itself into its mother's embrace? What a tender and loving scene this painting would depict! Everyone not only has no need to panic about this, but if they believe in auspicious omens, they should regard this as a celebratory omen. In the "Records of the Three Kingdoms," didn't Lady Wu dream of the moon entering her womb and then gave birth to Sun Ce? If a vague deer dream is already so effective, then if the bright moon truly throws itself into your embrace, the hero born in response to this auspicious sign will surely have a career far surpassing that of Sun Ce, who could only carve out a territory in Jiangdong.

Speaking of "Earth calling itself Mother," the phrase "Earth is the mother" is most appropriate when referring to the moon. If humans are not created by God, they must be born of parents. If the sun, moon, and stars are not created by God, then the sun, moon, and stars must also have their own parents. The difference is that human lifespans are exceptionally short, and we can trace back several generations. The lifespan of the sun, moon, and stars, compared to human lifespans, is far more than that of the giant *chun* tree, which considers five thousand years as spring and five thousand years as autumn, standing side-by-side with the ephemeral mayfly that lives for a single day. Therefore, the circumstances of their birth are already shrouded in the thick fog of a distant, ancient past. However, based on astronomical observations and the application of mathematical and physical principles, we can still find some clues to follow. But to trace back further, while scholars of astronomy and mathematics are unwilling to admit that they have reached the limit of their abilities, listeners cannot help but feel lost in a dense fog. Regarding the formation of the Earth and other planets in the solar system, the binary theory is currently the most dominant. Apart from lower animals like amoebas that can divide themselves to reproduce asexually, all other animals must rely on the cooperation of their parents to produce offspring. The sun's family is only able to have these nine major planets because, in the past, it must have met another sun (that is, a fixed star) and had a fleeting encounter, resulting in a temporary union. From the current situation where the sun is still working hard to nurture and raise these nine children, the sun is clearly an unfortunate abandoned woman. And that ungrateful and heartless stellar father has probably fled to the depths of the Milky Way to form a binary star again, and we have no way to pursue the matter further.

After all, there is a difference between the celestial and human realms. The circumstances of the sun giving birth must have been a magnificent sight. The power of the sun and moon is enough to cause huge tides on the surface of the Earth and in the oceans. When that enormous, unparalleled stellar father passed shoulder-to-shoulder with the sun, there must also have been an exceptionally unusual tidal force. Moreover, the sun is a hot ball of gas, unlike the Earth, which is so calm and stable. Therefore, the tides stirred up on the sun at that time were simply a torrent of surging hot liquid, shooting into the sky. This substance, thin at both ends and bulging in the middle, was subject to the gravitational pull of both the stellar father and the sun, and it broke apart to become these planets, orbiting the sun. At the same time, while the planets were still in an unsolidified state, they were influenced by the gravitational pull of other planets and the sun, and in the same way, they also produced many satellites. If the planets are the children of the sun, then the satellites are the grandchildren of the sun. However, the method of reproduction in the celestial realm is to give birth to sons and hold grandchildren at the same time, which can never be achieved in the human world.

Tragedy Occurs at Wuhu Wharf 86

(Wuhu) On the 1st at noon, the Japanese ship Daichimaru was loading iron sand in Wuhu when the wharf gangplank suddenly broke in the middle. More than thirty workers fell into the river. Only five people were rescued on the spot, and the rest tragically drowned. The cause of the accident was due to the rotten gangplank. The shipping affair was contracted by the Kin-kai Yusen Kaisha. Yellow River Water Rises in Four Counties of Xuzhou 88

(Xuzhou) The Yellow River water in the four counties of Xuzhou has been rising continuously. The continuous rainfall in recent days has increased the water level beyond the highest recorded level. Some embankments in Tongshan and Pei Counties are still under pressure, and there is a possibility of expanding the disaster area at any time. The new disaster area in Pei County is thirty *li* from north to south and fifty *li* from east to west. The waves are vast, villages are submerged, and houses are almost completely collapsed. People have all moved away. The slightly sprouted sorghum has been exhausted, and the wheat is damp and will not ignite. There are signs of food shortages in the wilderness. (Central News Agency dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Recently, large numbers of Japanese people have come to Xuzhou in an endless stream to tour. Many Koreans also accompanied them, carrying packages and suitcases. They refused roadside police inspection when getting off the train and behaved arrogantly. They also went to the city and suburbs to inspect and requested to take photographs. They stayed in Xuzhou for one or two days and then went to Bianliang and Zhengzhou, or returned to Jinan and Tianjin. According to a report from Haizhou, the number of Japanese people arriving in Lianyungang recently is endless. They claimed to be tourists. (Central News Agency dispatch)

Ancient Jar Full of Silver Ingots Discovered in Donghai 93

(Xuzhou) Farmers in Donghai County at the foot of Jinping Mountain discovered an ancient jar full of silver ingots while digging up tree roots. The estimated value is about 200 yuan. The ancient jar was broken, making it impossible to determine which dynasty it was from. However, the jar was filled with black mud, which sealed the silver ingots, so it was definitely not a modern item. (1st-day dispatch)

Japanese Troops Withdraw from Fengtai Song Zheyuan Still Declines New Post as Pacification Commissioner Japanese Troops Continuously Increase Garrison at Gubeikou Area Cheng Ke Arrives in Peiping to Discuss the Latest Situation in Tianjin 94

Peiping correspondence: The situation in North China seemed to ease slightly on the 28th and 29th, but it is still difficult to be optimistic. Song Zheyuan, the commander of the Peiping-Tianjin Garrison, expressed his humble refusal to accept the new post of Pacification Commissioner of Hebei-Chahar-Suiyuan to He Yingqin in a telegram. He immediately replied with a telegram of consolation. On the evening of the 28th, Song convened Qin Dechun, Xiao Zhenying, and others at his private residence in Wuyi Ku Hutong to discuss ways to seek stability in the current situation. He re-telegraphed He, earnestly requesting him to forward the message to the Central Government to withdraw the order. At the same time, he dispatched Liu Jialuan, a staff officer of the Peiping-Tianjin Garrison Headquarters, to Baoding as a representative to meet with Shang Zhen, the chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, urging Shang to come to Peiping immediately to discuss major plans. Liu also left Peiping southward that evening by the Peiping-Hankou train.

After returning to Taiyuan from Nanjing, Yan Xishan, the Pacification Commissioner of Taiyuan, telegraphed Fu Zuoyi, the chairman of the Suiyuan Provincial Government, and Xu Yongchang, the chairman of the Shanxi Provincial Government, to come to Taiyuan for discussions. Fu has already arrived in Taiyuan from Suiyuan. Xu, who was recuperating in Peiping, has recovered and also left Peiping on the night of the 28th to return to Shanxi. Song Zheyuan, Xiao Zhenying, Qin Dechun, and others went to see him off. It is reported that after Xu arrived in Taiyuan, in addition to reporting his recovery to Yan, he will also report on the recent situation in Hebei and the measures taken by the authorities. Xu is expected to come to Peiping again in the middle of next month.

A unit of Japanese troops, on the evening of the 28th, traveled in more than 40 large automobiles from Luanping to Gubeikou, disembarking on the east and west sides of the river and stationed in pre-designated civilian houses. The number of Japanese troops arriving this time was no more than two or three hundred, but the Japanese side claimed 500. It was also said that the Gubeikou area was insufficient for the Japanese troops to garrison, and the troops arriving later would live in the Shixia and Miyun areas. In addition, the Japanese troops newly arrived at Gubeikou from outside the pass have reached 1,000 artillery soldiers and 800 infantry soldiers. Although they claimed that they would advance south to Miyun and Huairou, they have not yet moved. The situation within the boundaries of Huairou and Miyun counties is still peaceful. More than 500 Japanese troops, who arrived at various passes along the Great Wall from units such as the Independent Mixed Brigade stationed in Rehe-Chifeng area, are busy running around by car every day. The Japanese troops originally stationed at Saheqiao had already moved to Zunhua and other counties on the 26th. One battalion of Japanese troops originally stationed in Dongling has gone to Xinglong and Malan airfield. There are many Japanese planes parked at the airfield, and they fly to various counties inside the pass every day for reconnaissance.

More than 100 Japanese soldiers went to the Fengtai and Guang'anmen railway stations on the 27th, claiming to monitor traffic. After negotiations between the Peiping authorities and the Japanese side, 80 Japanese soldiers withdrew from Fengtai at 9:45 a.m. on the 28th and returned to the Peiping barracks. The remaining ten or so soldiers stayed in Fengtai to guard the station. The Japanese soldiers at Guang'anmen railway station also withdrew entirely by car back to the Peiping Japanese barracks at 8:40 a.m. that morning. There were rumors that there were also Japanese soldiers in Changxindian. It was investigated that on the morning of the 27th, two Japanese people in plainclothes went to the station to inquire about traffic conditions and then left immediately. There were no Japanese troops going there. As for the Peiping-Liaoning, Peiping-Hankou, and Peiping-Suiyuan railways, passenger and freight trains operated as usual on the 28th.

Cheng Ke, the mayor of Tianjin, came to Peiping to visit Song Zheyuan, the commander of the Peiping-Tianjin Garrison, and discussed matters concerning Tianjin's security, the security team, and police command. According to Cheng, "The activities of the ignorant people in Tianjin have now been quelled. Several of the ringleaders have reportedly been sent outside the pass. However, the crisis still exists. Before I came to Peiping, I and Director Liu (Yushu) had made thorough arrangements for security. There should be no problems in the next three to five days. If the central government does not have a proper solution after that, I will feel extremely uneasy. The Japanese troops in Tianjin are building an airfield in Dongjuzi, which can accommodate many planes. It is said that 50 Japanese planes will fly to Tianjin and increase air force equipment. The Japanese side claims that this is an exercise, but the scale is larger than previous ones. The Japanese troops interfered with railway affairs at Tianjin-Pukou Railway Station. After I negotiated with the Japanese side, the misunderstanding has been cleared up, so traffic has not been obstructed. I came to Peiping to visit Commander Song to discuss ways to maintain Tianjin's security. In the future, I will be responsible for diplomacy, while Song will be responsible for security. Dividing the work and cooperating will be better than having one person responsible for everything alone." (November 29)

Wuhan Press Telegraphs Central Government to Suppress Traitors and Telegraphs Military and Political Authorities in North China to Protect Territory, Soliciting Joint Telegraphs from Colleagues to All Countries to Uphold Justice 95

Hankou correspondence: Yin Rugeng's rebellious actions in eastern Hebei, betraying the motherland, and the Fengtai Incident have provoked indignation among the people of Wuhan. The entire press held a meeting today and decided on the following measures: 1. Telegraph the Central Government and the National Government, urging them to make a prompt decision to quickly quell the rebellion. 2. Telegraph the military and political leaders of North China, urging them to protect the territory and sovereignty. 3. Telegraph colleagues across the country to turn to compatriots across the country to strictly prevent the activities of traitors and rise up together to relieve the national crisis. And solicit joint telegraphs from colleagues across the country to the League of Nations and authorities of various countries to uphold justice and maintain peace. Three telegraphs were sent that evening, as follows: (1) Telegram to the Central Government and National Government: "Unfortunately, the country is suffering from repeated disasters. It is the duty of every citizen to save the country and survive. Yin Rugeng has recently rebelled in eastern Hebei, encroaching on North China, threatening the survival of the nation. All those with blood and spirit are filled with sorrow and despair. We believe that like cutting off a snake-bitten hand, a prompt decision should be made to quickly quell the rebellion, stabilize North China, protect sovereignty, and secure the territory. We make this urgent appeal, hoping you will consider it." Wuhan press collectively kowtows. (2) Telegraph to the military and political leaders of various provinces in North China: "Unfortunately, the country is suffering from repeated disasters. It is the duty of every citizen to save the country and survive. Yin Rugeng has recently rebelled in eastern Hebei, encroaching on North China, threatening the survival of the nation. All those with blood and spirit are filled with sorrow and despair. You are sitting in Peiping and Tianjin, the key to the northern gate, and you have an unshirkable responsibility to protect the territory. We urge you to exert all your efforts to quickly quell the rebellion, and we hope you will not have any reservations. If you leave endless troubles, all our citizens will share the same hatred and stand together as a backup, not hesitating to make any sacrifices. We make this urgent appeal, hoping you will consider it." Wuhan press collectively kowtows. (3) Telegram to colleagues and compatriots across the country: "To colleagues across the country and compatriots across the country, the nation is unfortunately facing continuous rebellions. It is the duty of every craftsman to save the country and survive. Yin Rugeng, as an official responsible for defending the country, dares to rebel and instigate chaos in eastern Hebei, encroaching on North China, threatening the survival of the nation. We are aware of the urgency of the situation and have gathered today to telegraph the Central Government, urging them to make a prompt decision to quickly quell the rebellion, stabilize North China, protect sovereignty, and secure the territory, and to telegraph the local officials in Peiping and Tianjin, urging them to quickly quell the rebellion without any reservations. All citizens share the same hatred and stand together as a backup. This has been unanimously approved on record. The current situation is becoming increasingly serious. We propose that your colleagues unanimously advocate and work together for a solution. We also hope to guide the public to be vigilant against the activities of traitors at all times to avoid them taking advantage of the chaos. The country will be fortunate, and the nation will be fortunate." Wuhan press collectively kowtows. As for the telegram to colleagues across the country soliciting a joint telegram to the League of Nations and authorities of various countries, Xie Chuheng, Wang Yaming, and Li Xiaomei were designated to draft it, and it will be issued after being reviewed by Lin Rongkui, Ding Wenan, Liu Zhiping, and Bi Chengjun. (November 28)

Kong Xiangrong Talks About the Dongzhuang Dike Closing Problem Materials to be Transported Within a Month Dam to be Closed Next Spring Light Railway of 20 Li to be Laid for Earth Transport 96

Jinan correspondence: Regarding the Dongzhuang Yellow River dike closing project, it has been approved by the National Economic Commission and transferred from the provincial dike closing work committee to the Yellow River Conservancy Commission for continued handling. Kong Xiangrong, the acting chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, is currently in Jinan and is in close contact with the dike closing work committee to handle the transfer procedures. According to him, regarding the transfer of the Dongzhuang Yellow River dike closing project to the commission, Provincial Director Zhang Honglie had repeatedly pleaded with him beforehand, stating the real situation that he could not go to the worksite to command. It was not until 10:00 p.m. yesterday (the 28th) that he received the telegram from the Economic Commission relayed from Kaifeng ordering the acceptance of the project. The commission and the local authorities have always had a harmonious relationship, and all contacts have been open and honest. Since the Yellow River breach, Chairman Han and Director Zhang have planned day and night for dike closing and disaster relief, and resettlement of disaster victims, sparing no effort, which is admirable. However, Chairman Han and Director Zhang are busy with government affairs and cannot go to the worksite to command. He, as the person responsible for Yellow River management, has an unshirkable duty for the dike closing project. However, the dike closing project is huge and still requires local assistance and joint efforts. After the commission takes over, it will continue according to the original plan. The materials can only be checked and accepted according to the actual existing quantity to ensure that the project is not interrupted for a single day. A detailed handover book must be created later. As for whether there will be any changes in the engineering office, it is still not possible to determine at present. He must personally go to the worksite to inspect before studying it. However, the project is important, and the current director is Director Zhang (Lianjia) of the River Affairs Bureau, who has been very hardworking in the past. The River Affairs Bureau will still be asked to assist in the future. The current Yellow River water situation has reached the level of the entire river vying for the flow. The Jiangsus dam leading flow project is important, and it is planned to concentrate efforts to complete this project, recover part of the main flow, reduce the flood water, so that the flood water only flows into the already scoured trough, does not overflow, and reduces the disaster area. At a minimum, we will first provide relief to some of the disaster victims. The new dam foundation will also be carried out at the same time. Materials are the main items for the project. According to the original plan for the entire project, there are 17,000 cubic meters of stone and 6,000 stacks of straw. Currently, 5,000 cubic meters of stone have arrived at the worksite. In addition to the 1,000 cubic meters that have been used, more than 12,000 cubic meters are still needed. About 1,000 stacks of straw have arrived at the worksite, and more than 4,000 stacks are still needed. The transport of earth is even more difficult. There is no surplus at the worksite. Once the weather turns cold, it will be difficult to extract soil, and frozen soil is not suitable for the project. It is necessary to concentrate efforts and actively transport the soil, aiming to transport all the materials within a month, so that the dam can be closed next spring and not delay spring plowing, because the Economic Commission originally set a deadline for closing the dam in April. Although closing the dam before the ice flood is ahead of schedule, it is difficult to ensure solidity when working in winter, and the scouring force of the ice flood is great, so there will be losses. For material transport, on the one hand, increase the number of large boats hired in Henan and Hebei, designating them to transport stone and straw separately, and designate the allocated trains to be dedicated to transporting stone. For the transport of other materials, please temporarily allocate vehicles to avoid delaying the transport of stone. The straw will be entrusted to the counties along the river in Shandong, Henan, and Hebei to purchase quickly. On the other hand, plan to lay a light railway track on both banks of the new river to transport earth. It is planned to set up one round-trip road on each bank, about four or five *hua li* long, so that new soil can be extracted. A total of ten to twenty *li* of track can be used. Also, raise dozens of dump trucks for transportation back and forth to pile up the soil at the worksite for temporary use. As for the problem of mortgaging 3 million disaster relief bonds, it is also planned to quickly find a way to mortgage them for cash to meet urgent needs. He plans to return to Kaifeng to inspect Dongzhuang once after discussing the handover method with Chairman Han and Director Zhang today, arrange the project affairs properly, and then go to Nanjing to report and negotiate everything mentioned above. After completing the work, he will return to Dongzhuang and stay at the worksite permanently to supervise the progress. The dike closing meeting will be set up in Dongzhuang in order to facilitate matters. The project cost budget will remain the same for the time being, but we will strive to save money when it is actually used, so that the funds will not be wasted.

Recent Developments in Southern Jiangxi Construction Yu Hanmou's Report on Returning to Guangdong 97

Guangzhou correspondence: The current situation is serious, and the defenses are extremely important. In order to understand the defenses of the troops stationed in various places, Chen Jitang convened the army commanders, division commanders, and brigade commanders of his troops back to the province to consult on everything. Those who have returned to the province in recent days include division commanders Zhang Ruigui, Ye Zhao, Huang Zhiwen, Deng Longguang, and Li Hanhun. Around the 20th, Li Yangjing, the commander of the Third Army, and Yu Hanmou, the commander of the First Army, also returned to the province from their defense areas successively. Meetings were held starting on the 23rd, and discussions were held on the equipment for naval, air, and land defense, the distribution of troops, the reorganization of national defense fortresses, and the progress of pacification. A complete plan was drawn up. On the 25th, Yu Hanmou, the commander of the First Army, reported on the recent situation of pacification and construction in southern Jiangxi at the weekly memorial service of the Southwest Political Affairs Council, stating that after Zhu Mao's communist bandits fled westward, the First Army sent teams to pacify southern Jiangxi. The remnants of the bandits were gradually cleared. Until September of this year, the Southern Jiangxi Pacification Commissioner's Office was ordered to be abolished. Until recently, a small group of bandits was discovered on the Hunan border, and Peng, the commander of the First Division, was sent with troops to suppress them. According to recent reports, the bandit group has been dispersed, and more than 20 hostages have been rescued. He inspected the local situation in the Xinfeng and Anyuan areas at the beginning of the month and saw that the countryside was gradually recovering, and most of the wasteland had been cultivated. When the communist bandits fled, there was often panic about food in southern Jiangxi. Because the farmland has been harvested, there is no need to worry about lack of food. However, in order to prevent poor harvests, we have promoted winter plowing, built warehouses, and stored grain to prepare for lean years. After the bandit disaster in the three southern counties, the schools were closed, and the people's wisdom was backward. Recently, the First Rural Normal School was established in Dayu, and the Second Rural Normal School was established in Longnan. One class of students from the First Rural Normal School graduated this spring and were assigned to various townships to run civilian schools and primary schools. As for the construction of highways, it is the main construction of the area. The highways from Xunwu and Longchuan to Pingyuan, Dingnan to Heping, and Qiannan to Wengyuan have been built and opened to traffic. As for the roads from Xinfeng to Anyuan and Xinfeng to Longnan, they are still under construction. The Shuiche Bridge in Xinfeng and the Jing'an Bridge in Dayu are temporarily built with wood due to limited funds. Dayu has recently opened two new urban areas and built a bus terminal for the Gan-Yu-Xiong-Sou highways. The Commemorative Monument for Suppressing Bandits and the Martyrs' Cemetery and Martyrs' Shrine for the Fallen Soldiers in Suppressing Bandits have also been built. As for the financial aspects, southern Jiangxi is originally poor, and the money supply is not very abundant. Since the Central Government announced the use of legal currency, silver dollars have been gradually withdrawn, but prices are higher than before." (November 26)

Suzhou: Only Three Couples at the Group Wedding 98

The first group wedding initiated by the New Life Promotion Association of Wuxian County was originally scheduled to be held on the Double Tenth Festival. However, because there were few participants, it was postponed to 10:00 a.m. on the 1st at the Zhongshan Hall. Only three couples participated, and all the brides were women from the Women's Relief Center. The officiants were Sun Danchen and Peng Jiazhi, the master of ceremonies was Zhang Peng, and the Wuping Music Troupe was responsible for the music. Many guests came. It did not end until around 11:00 a.m. If the first time is so difficult, there is no day for a second time.

Wuxi: Fireworks Prohibited During Winter Defense Period 99

The First Office of the Wuxi County Winter Defense held its first meeting at the Public Security Bureau yesterday. The chairman was Chen Yuchu. It was resolved that: 1. The dates and locations for the joint patrol of the current winter defense period with the second, third, fourth, and fifth defense districts will be drafted. 2. More Than Ten Silk Factories Close Down One After Another 100

In our county, various silk factories are closing down one after another due to the rising price of dried cocoons and the shortage of raw materials. In addition to the five factories of Yonghua, Baisi, Wanchang, Xinchang, and Yichang, which have been closed for a long time, another five factories, including Heji, Yuanfongsheng, Xinda, Minsheng, and Gongda, have been forced to close down in the past half month. However, the Minsheng and Gongda factories have been in a stalemate due to labor-capital disputes arising from the distribution of bonuses. Recently, the overseas silk market has turned sluggish, and the price of high-quality white silk has fallen to 730-740 yuan per package. The market price of dried cocoons has also fallen from 225 yuan per dan to 180 yuan. The future of the silk market seems to be returning to a gloomy state.

Changzhou: Establishment of the Second Branch of the Narcotics Offenders Prison 101

Li Yurui, a prison supervisor in Wu County, believed that the prison was overcrowded after Zhu Shusen, the former President of the High Court, came to Changzhou for inspection, and that it was urgent to alleviate the congestion. He proposed the establishment of a second sub-prison for narcotics offenders to house the detained narcotics offenders separately. After consultation with the county government, the Yaowang Temple was selected as the site, and a budget was drawn up and submitted for approval to be allocated from the anti-narcotics funds. Up to now, all preparations have been completed, and the branch was officially established on December 1st. Narcotics offenders will be transferred to the branch, which can accommodate two to three hundred people.

Nantong: Thorough Investigation of Illegal Collection of Flag Fees 102

During the fishing season, sea bandits harassed and extorted fishing households in various coastal areas of Jiangbei, charging so-called flag fees, ranging from 30 to 50 yuan per boat, collecting a huge sum of more than 200,000 yuan over the years. However, even after the suppression of the sea bandits, some people continued to collect flag fees in the name of the water police. The Third District Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police arrested the ringleader, Zhang Futang, and implicated Wu Yanjie, the captain of the Twelfth Brigade. The District Department handed Zhang and Wu over to the Nantong District Court for thorough investigation. Zhang Futang was detained, and Wu Yanjie was released on bail. On the 29th, the Prosecutor's Office summoned Zhang Yunhui, chairman of the Lvsi Fishermen's Association, and others for questioning.

Hangzhou: Reorganization of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau 105

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau expects that the Yushan-Nanchang section of the project will be fully completed and open to traffic this month, and has ordered a large number of locomotives and passenger cars from Germany for use in Hangzhou. Luhe: Stranded Japanese Warship Has Escaped Danger 106

A Japanese warship stranded near the Jiang'an River bank near the Yongli Sulfuric Acid Factory in Xiejia Township in this county. Efforts to rescue it have failed, and it has been stranded for many days. It has been heard that the warship was able to float completely at 7:00 PM on the 28th. Due to the sudden change in weather, the strong northeast wind, and the surging waves, the Jiang'an River water suddenly flooded, and the stranded Japanese warship took advantage of the situation to open full power, reversed to the center of the river, and turned downstream, thus escaping the danger.

Jiaxing: Detained Meat Merchants Still Not Released 107

Meat merchants in Jiaxing have been detained by the county magistrate for failing to pay the additional slaughter tax, and it has been many days now without their release. The county chamber of commerce has repeatedly petitioned the county to change the additional tax to 50% and to release the detained meat merchants first. Since the tax is collected from the local people and used for local purposes, they should actively pay it. Why should they resist with excuses? Moreover, the additional tax is actually collected from the buyers, and the meat merchants are only responsible for collecting it on their behalf. They must wait until the tax is paid in full before they can be released. The request is temporarily rejected.

President Wang Resigns from All Concurrent Positions; Yesterday He Telegraphs the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee and Chairman Lin, and Simultaneously Sends Telegrams to the Heads of Various Ministries and Commissions. 108

According to the Central News Agency, President Wang's back injury has improved well after undergoing surgery performed by the Niu doctors the morning before. Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, came to Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning to visit President Wang's condition. According to his conversation with the Central News Agency reporter, President Wang is recovering well after the surgery, but because of prolonged illness and surgery, he needs a long period of rest to recover. President Wang specifically telegraphed the Fifth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee and Chairman Lin yesterday, earnestly requesting approval to resign from the positions of President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Foreign Affairs. At the same time, he telegraphed Acting President Kong and the heads of various ministries and commissions, stating that this was purely because his personal health could not support the burden, and that his colleagues were responsible for the country, so there was absolutely no joint responsibility. We now find the original telegrams recorded below.

Telegram to the First Plenary Session of the Central Committee: Nanjing Fifth Central Executive Committee First Plenary Session, Respectfully Submitted: Zhaoming has been injured for a month, with wounds on his cheeks and arms, which have gradually healed. However, the back wound has not healed, and surgery was performed again yesterday. Furthermore, after a serious illness in the autumn, the injury has become worse, and my physical strength feels even weaker. If I continue to hold heavy responsibilities, even though my own life is not worth regretting, it would be regrettable to delay national affairs. Therefore, I earnestly request approval to resign from the positions of President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Foreign Affairs. I will serve when my health is recovered. I respectfully request your inspection. Wang Zhaoming, East.

Telegram to Chairman Lin: Nanjing National Government Chairman Lin, Respectfully Submitted: Zhaoming has been injured for a month, with wounds on his cheeks and arms, which have gradually healed. However, the back wound has not healed, and surgery was performed again yesterday. Furthermore, after a serious illness in the autumn, the injury has become worse, and my physical strength feels even weaker. If I continue to hold heavy responsibilities, even though my own life is not worth regretting, it would be regrettable to delay national affairs. Therefore, I earnestly request approval to resign from the positions of President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Foreign Affairs. I will serve when my health is recovered. In addition to the telegram to the Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, I respectfully request your inspection. Wang Zhaoming, East.

Telegram to the Heads of Various Ministries and Commissions: Nanjing Executive Yuan Acting President, Minister Huang of the Ministry of Interior, Acting Minister Tao of the Ministry of [unclear], Acting Minister Xu of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Minister He of the Ministry of Military Affairs, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Navy, Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education, Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Transportation, Minister Gu of the Ministry of Railways, Chairman Huang of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, Chairman Chen of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, Director Liu of the Health Administration, Greetings: Because my injuries and illness have not healed, I have recently telegraphed the Central Executive Committee of the National Government to request the resignation of concurrent positions. This is purely because my personal health cannot support the burden, and that my colleagues are responsible for the country, so there is absolutely no joint responsibility. Recalling the four years of working together, I have received your teachings and benefits with my dull qualifications. I express my sincere thanks and respectfully request your inspection, and please convey my regards to all my colleagues. Wang Zhaoming, East.

Central, China, and Communications Banks Handle Interbank Overdrafts to Supplement Silver and Money Businesses and Indirectly Relieve Industry and Commerce; Money Business Representatives to Hold Meeting Today to Receive Legal Tender 111

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, after the Central, China, and Communications Banks were ordered by the Ministry of Finance to handle interbank overdrafts to relieve industry and commerce, silver and money businesses can borrow from the three banks in accordance with the regulations set by the Ministry. The money business will receive vouchers after the representatives' standing committee approves it today. The details are as follows:

Three Banks Ordered: After the Central, China, and Communications Banks were ordered, they decided to handle interbank overdrafts in accordance with the method of interbank lending during the closing of accounts in 1934 and at the end of April 1935. Xi Demao, Director of the Business Bureau of the Central Bank, Bei Songsun, Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the China Bank, and Zhang Peishen, Manager of the Business Bureau of the Communications Bank, jointly decided that the Business Bureau of the Central Bank will be responsible for the overdraft. The total amount of the overdraft will be determined according to market needs, and the three banks will share the amount according to the 4-4-2 system. The daily interbank interest rate will be announced daily, but it will be slightly lower than the ordinary rate. Although its direct purpose is to assist silver and money businesses, it is indirectly to relieve industry and commerce.

Two Businesses Comply: After the Ministry of Finance approved silver and money businesses to receive legal tender from the Central, China, and Communications Banks with 60% cash and 40% reserves, member banks of the Banking Association have complied one after another. Member shops of the Money Business Association have decided to send reserves to the United Reserve Bank in accordance with the resolution of the Executive Committee of the Association, and the cash previously paid to the three banks will be issued by the Bank to the three banks, and it is scheduled to hold a meeting of members' representatives at the Association on Ningbo Road at 2:00 PM today. It will be implemented after the approval of the earth's methods.

Maintain the Financial Industry in Jiangxi Province; Loan Negotiation Successful; Amount of 3.4 Million, Interest Rate and Term to Be Determined Separately; Director Wu Jiantao of the Jiangxi Provincial Department of Finance Returned to Jiangxi Yesterday to Report 112

According to the Central News Agency, in order to rescue the banks and money shops in Jiangxi Province and seek the revival of industry and commerce, the Jiangxi Provincial Government specially sent Wu Jiantao, Director of the Provincial Department of Finance, to Shanghai several days ago to visit Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi for instructions, and to visit Vice Minister Xu and the persons in charge of the Central, China, and Communications Banks to discuss. It is heard that a result has been negotiated, and the Central, China, and Communications Banks will provide loans of 3.4 million yuan through the branches of the three banks in Jiangxi, using the 38 money shops in the province as jointly responsible guarantors, in accordance with the method of interbank lending in Shanghai. A review committee will be organized by representatives from the Department of Finance and seven banks, including the Central China Communications Jiangxi Yumin Banks, to preside over the matter. The loan interest rate and term will be determined and announced by the committee based on local conditions and market supply and demand. Its nature is the same as the interbank lending in Shanghai. Its role is directly to maintain the money business, and indirectly to develop industry and commerce and revive the social economy. Because the negotiation had results, Wu returned to the province yesterday to report.

Life insurance below 50 to 500 yuan, whether individual or group, belongs to the scope of simple life insurance, temporarily divided into two types: whole life insurance and term insurance (term insurance is further divided into 10-year, 15-year, 20-year, and 25-year insurance). All business personnel have also completed the examination and are specially responsible for handling it. All postal savings and remittance branches and post offices in this city can undertake it. Detailed regulations can be obtained from the Bureau.

Mr. Manley Discusses the Future of the Philippine Republic; What He Discusses Is Unheard of by People in Shanghai 120

According to the Mainland News, Mr. Manley, an official of the Washington office of the Chicago Tribune, who went to Manila to participate in the founding ceremony of the new Philippine Republic, has arrived in Shanghai and talked to a reporter from the Mainland News about Philippine affairs, much of which is unheard of by people in Shanghai. It is said that in the days before the election in the Philippines, the situation in Manila was very tense. It was rumored that the defeated presidential candidate, Mr. Oquinaldo, would launch a rebellion. Oquinaldo had initially engaged in fraudulent activities in the election. According to insiders, the American Governor-General Murphy visited Oquinaldo the day before the ceremony and asked him if he was going to do anything. Oquinaldo told Murphy that he planned to lead 60,000 of his followers into Manila on the day of the ceremony. Oquinaldo was very popular among civil servants and received 200,000 votes in this election, while Quezon received 800,000 votes. Murphy advised Oquinaldo not to take any rash actions that would damage the reputation of the Philippines, which would be unwise from various standpoints. Oquinaldo followed his advice and did not take any action. This statement seems quite credible, because no incident occurred afterwards, and Oquinaldo did not even attend the ceremony. Another thing is also quite relevant, that is, Quezon slept on the American cruiser the night before taking office as president. Mr. Manley believes that the departure of the American congressional delegation from Manila has raised doubts about whether the Philippine Republic's plan will succeed in the future. Most members of Congress feel that the United States will return to the Philippines or completely abandon it within a few years. American merchants are strongly opposed to allowing the Philippines to become independent, while American farmers are more in favor of it because their products can reduce competition. As for the average Filipinos, most of them do not know the meaning of independence, and politicians naturally support the Republican plan. However, Filipino businessmen are quite worried about the future. Filipinos must survive on the basis of preferential tax rates. At first, it was thought that preferential trade agreements could be concluded with various countries, including the United States, but now it seems difficult for these trade agreements to become a reality, so the economic life of the Philippines will be greatly distressed. The public does not express any fear about the security of the Philippines, especially against Japan. However, the public believes that the United States will come forward to protect the Philippines when it needs help. Quezon once said that he planned to train an army to prevent troublemakers from daring to take advantage. The size of the army is set at 19,000 people. You can decide for yourselves how effective this army will be. Mr. Manley is currently staying at the American Association and plans to go to Japan in the next few days for a short stay, and then plans to return to his country. Mr. Manley is a graduate of the journalism department of the University of Missouri.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Continues to Release Interpretations of Stamp Tax Doubts - A Total of Thirty-Two Cases 126

Since the implementation of the new stamp tax, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, based on requests from various trade associations or shops to resolve stamp tax doubts, has successively released more than seventy interpretations. Now, the association has released thirty-two interpretations, all based on the Ministry's approvals and tax regulations for guidance. The full text is published in the 11th issue of the 15th volume of the Chamber of Commerce's monthly magazine. The solutions to each case are recorded as follows: (1) The Ministry approves that shareholder registers, stock affairs record books, etc., are exempt from stamp tax. (2) The Ministry approves that delivery slips used by the transit industry should be affixed with stamps. (3) The Ministry approves that decoction instructions should be affixed with stamps. (4) The Ministry approves that red account bills do not need to be affixed with stamps. (5) The Ministry approves that detailed item prices listed on delivery slips should be affixed with stamps. (6) Delivery slips that also serve as receipts should be stamped according to the receipt regulations. (7) Goods temporary record books should be affixed with stamps. (8) Sales report forms should be changed to invoice stubs. (9) Work passes are exempt from stamp tax, but workbooks established by factories cannot be exempted. (10) Labor cards used for paying wages do not need to be affixed with stamps. (11) Delivery slips issued by the business department to the goods room do not need to be affixed with stamps. (12) The responsibility for affixing stamps to order forms lies with the person issuing the order. (13) Warehouse receipts should be affixed with stamps according to the consignment receipt regulations. (14) Vouchers used in commerce are not within the scope of the treasury and should be affixed with stamps. (15) There are no explicit provisions in the law for affixing stamps to correspondence related to banking transactions. (16) The distinction between stamp duty on savings receipts and deposit receipts. (17) Drafts of correspondence between merchants do not need to be affixed with stamps. (18) Delivery slips, being invoices, should be affixed with stamps. (19) Blank invoices should be stamped according to the invoice regulations. (20) Employee merit/demerit and leave books do not need to be affixed with stamps. (21) An explanation that receipts for association membership fees should be affixed with stamps. (22) Except for receipts, organization account books do not need to be affixed with stamps. (23) Donation books of charitable organizations are exempt from stamp tax, but receipts should be affixed with stamps. (24) According to the law, soy sauce shop delivery slips do not need to be affixed with stamps. (25) Stamp tax measures for the pig industry's account books and records. (26) Applications for purchasing official contract paper are exempt from stamp tax. (27) Licenses for pharmacists, midwives, etc., will be changed to a single stamp of 50 cents in the future according to law. (28) In cases of penalties for violating the stamp tax law, the original inspection and investigation agency may file an appeal. (29) Appeals against stamp tax penalties should be filed by the punished store. (30) Account books used by individuals or families, regardless of their content, must be affixed with stamps. (31) The Judicial Yuan interprets doubts regarding stamp tax penalty incidents. (32) Checks issued by government agencies are exempt from stamp tax.

Customs Exempts Dredging Tax: Directly Reduces the Burden on Domestic Merchants and Indirectly Helps Increase Exported Goods 128

According to the National News Agency, the dredging tax has always been collected by the Customs, i.e., 3 taels are added to every 100 taels of customs tax, and tax-exempt goods are subject to a levy of 1 tael and 5 mace per 10 taels of value. The Director of the Shanghai Dredging Bureau believes that at a time when southern industries are declining and the government is showing concern for merchants' difficulties, customs duties on exported domestic goods are being considered for separate reductions and exemptions, while this tax is still being collected as usual, which is contrary to the government's good intentions. Furthermore, the dredging project was originally intended to develop port affairs, and the decline of local goods is particularly important to the future of port affairs. Therefore, exempting this tax would directly reduce the burden on domestic merchants and encourage the increase of exported goods, while indirectly seeking the development of port affairs. He submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to exempt all tax-exempt exported goods and domestic goods exported in the future from dredging tax for a trial period of one year to observe the results. This has been approved by the Ministry of Finance and instructed the Jianghai Customs to comply accordingly.

The Monologue Improvement Association Discusses and Decides on Four Prohibitions and Two Requirements Yesterday 135

According to the Shanghai News Agency, comic monologues are a newly emerging art form with a history of only a few decades. The actors engaged in this art form have also been neglected by society. However, because the content and organization of this art form are extremely simple, and the singing is as humorous as possible, it is quite popular among the public. In recent years, it has become extremely popular. Such as the late Wang Wuneng, and the current Jiang Xiaoxiao, Liu Chunshan, Zhuang Yanghua, Lu Qiqi, Zhao Xixi, Cheng Xiaoting, etc. broadcasting on various radio stations, almost all citizens of the city know about them. From this, it can be seen that the power of this art form has penetrated into the people. Pan, the director of the Municipal Education Bureau, wants to use this art form as a tool to promote social education, and specially sent Ding Shoutang, the drama and song record review committee member of the bureau, to lead the city's monologue actors to organize the Shanghai Comic Monologue Research Association. Ding himself served as the executive director, which can not only increase the status of monologue actors in society, but also enable all actors to earnestly improve their lyrics, so as to achieve the effect of imperceptible influence. Yesterday was the seventh regular meeting of the association. It is learned that there are four prohibitions and two musts in the important resolutions. The four prohibitions are to eliminate negative effects. The six specific methods for improving monologues are determined to improve the content of monologues to assist social education. All members of the Shanghai Comic Monologue Research Association should abide by them. If there is any violation, it will be reported to the Municipal Education Bureau for severe punishment. (1) It is not allowed to sing or perform obscene words and sentences, such as "軋姘頭" (having an affair), "吊膀子" (flirting), etc., and actions related to public morals. (2) It is not allowed to have abusive sentences, such as "赤老" (old fart), "觸　娘" (cursing someone's mother), "癟三" (bum), etc. (3) It is not allowed to sing sad tunes, such as crying for Wang Wuneng, Ding Guai Guai, and Sun Yat-sen. (4) It is not allowed to sing or perform words and tunes that the authorities have already banned, such as imitating "毛毛雨" (drizzle), "桃花江調" (Peach Blossom River tune), and the grass skirt dance, etc. B. Two necessities in the active aspect: (1) All members, whether performing on stage or at radio stations, must insert a section of singing with social benefits and educational significance in each performance or broadcast. (2) All members must completely copy the lyrics into a book and submit them to the Education Bureau for review.

Residents of Sidali on Shigaota Road Demand Rent Reduction 136

Since last year, due to the economic downturn, houses along North Sichuan Road Shigaota Road have been successively reducing rents. This time, the tenants of Sidali on Shigaota Road were frightened by the rumors and panic, and the timid ones moved away one after another. Although the rumors have subsided recently, the residents are like frightened birds, and new tenants who want to inquire about the area next to the headquarters of the Japanese Marines have a sense of caution. Therefore, the area has become a bleak scene. It is estimated that less than a quarter of the tenants in the entire area are currently living there. Recently, they have united to ask the landlord to waive the rent for November and December of this year and to reduce the rent by half starting from January next year. It is heard that the landlord of this area has always had a good income, and this time he has also shown conscience, sympathized with the difficulties of the times, and is happy to accept the tenant's request. The document of the tenants of this area requesting the landlord Hengli Company is copied as follows: "Respectful greetings, since last year, the market has been in decline, and landlords everywhere who are considerate of the difficulties of the times have automatically reduced rents to ease the plight of tenants. We have been busy with our duties and have not had time to negotiate with your landlord, and have paid the rent as usual every month, in the hope that your landlord would realize it himself, but your landlord has turned a deaf ear, procrastinating until now, with no expression of sympathy. Now that rumors have arisen, and people have moved away from the empty alleys, the once prosperous area has suddenly become a remote village, with few lights and little smoke, a desolate scene, and it is felt that restoration is difficult. The losses we have suffered are equal to those of a disaster. In the past, we were able to barely support ourselves by subletting to others to make up for the losses, but now nine out of ten rooms are empty, and no one cares about the rest. It is even more difficult to bear the burden alone. We and your landlord have been guests and hosts for many years, interdependent, and we have never followed the trend to make things difficult for the landlord. At this critical time, we have to discuss ways to save the future. It has now been decided to ask your landlord to waive the rent for November and December of this year, and to reduce the rent by half starting from January until the city returns to its original state. This method is not an excessive request. It is believed that your landlord is aware of the times and will resolutely agree, without the need to bargain back and forth, and the time will be delayed, and both parties will suffer losses. Please reply in writing within ten days, and please send a letter to the Finance Bureau to handle the housing donation in proportion. We will pay the rent on time after receiving your reply. The matter concerns maintaining the overall situation of the market, and your landlord has an inescapable duty. Please send the letter to the temporary office of the Tenants Association in this area. Sincerely, the Tenants of Sidali."

Yarn Mill King's Scandal with Famous Socialite: A Tragedy Amidst Industrial and Commercial Decline, a Change in the Battle Between Golden Women 150

Miss Zhou is the niece of General Li, who is currently in retirement. She recently returned from studying abroad in America, her attire is fashionable, her behavior extravagant, and those she associates with are all gentry and celebrities. Because of this, her reputation has risen and she has become a socialite. When General Li was in power, the current Yarn Mill King received much assistance from him. Therefore, the Yarn Mill King still feels grateful for General Li's support, and the two have a close friendship. Later, Miss Zhou grew tired of the social scene and wanted to find a place to settle down. She asked her uncle, General Li, to help her become the Yarn Mill King's English secretary. According to the real situation of the case reported yesterday, which stated that the suicide of Zhao Dexiong, the general manager of the Zhenxing Yarn Mill, was related to the socialite Miss Zhou Manli, Miss Zhou was merely Zhao Dexiong's "trophy wife."
